# Apple

# Description __

An Apple. Eating it provides a small boost to health, hunger, and thirst.

Page views: 3,503  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Rotten Apple

# Description __

A rotten apple. Eating it currently provides a tiny boost to health, hunger, and thirst.

Page views: 2,721  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Chippy Arcade Game

# Description __

An Arcade Machine

## Crafting Costs __

  * x10 High Quality Metal
  * x2 Gear



## Recycling Output __

  * x5 High Quality Metal
  * x1 Gear

# Bone Arrow

# Description __

An Arrow equipped with a large bone arrowhead making it very easy to hit targets at the expense of damage. Ammunition for: Bow, Crossbow, Compound Bow.

Page views: 6,612  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Fire Arrow

# Description __

A fuel soaked arrow, ignite it by aiming into a fire source.

Page views: 7,660  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# High Velocity Arrow

# Description __

Lighter, faster arrow that deals less damage.

# Bunny Onesie

# Description __

A Bunny Onesie. Grants additional Egg Vision allowing you to detect more eggs during an Easter egg hunt.

Page views: 5,535  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Bunny Ears

# Description __

Bunny Ears. Grants additional Egg Vision allowing you to detect more eggs during an Easter egg hunt.

Page views: 3,486  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

  * [ __History](/rust/item/autoturret~history)



# Auto Turret

# Description __

This automated electric sentry turret will engage and neutralize any moving targets it has line of sight to. You must equip it with a projectile weapon and the corresponding ammunition. Note : The turret will search for targets in a 180 degree arc facing _you_ when you place it. Requires 10 power.

Page views: 13,999  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Salvaged Axe

# Description __

A high-yield resource gathering axe. Slower than the Hatchet.

Page views: 4,920  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

#  [Rust Wiki](/rust/)

[Home](/rust/) / [Bandage](/rust/item/bandage)

  * [ __View](/rust/item/bandage)
  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/bandage~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/bandage~history)



# Bandage

# Description __

Heal yourself or others with this bandage. Left-click heals you, right-click heals a target.

The purpose of Bandages is chiefly to treat and prevent damage due to blood loss.

Most physical damage in Rust causes some degree of "Bleeding", indicated by the status effect and value above your health/hunger/thirst bars. Bleeding causes additional damage over time, indicated by the level of the effect, and suppresses healing effects such as the +20 healing from a Medical Syringe. Bandages can treat a significant amount of this, and as such, are best used alongside other healing items, e.g. Medical Syringe, to ensure they can be used effectively.

A bandage takes 4 cloth to craft and is a default blueprint.

Healing |   
---|---  
Health | +5  
Healing | 0  
Hydration | 0  
Bleeding | -50  
Radiation | 0  
Poison | -2  
  
It takes 5 seconds to craft a Bandage.

Page views: 4,819  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Concrete Barricade

# Description __

A barricade made out of Stones.

# Crafting Costs __

x300 Stones

Page views: 3,556  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/barricade.metal~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/barricade.metal~history)



# Metal Barricade

# Description __

A tough metal barricade with barbed wire, made from Metal Fragments. The barbed wire causes damage and will also slow player movement.

# Crafting Costs __

x200 Metal Fragments x2 Metal blade

Page views: 4,594  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Sandbag Barricade

# Description __

A protective barricade made out of Sand Bags.

# Crafting __

Items | Quantity  
---|---  
Cloth | X10  
Stones | X100  
  
Page views: 3,112  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Stone Barricade

# Description __

A protective barricade made out of Stones.

Page views: 3,087  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Wooden Barricade

# Description __

A wooden barricade. Will hurt players and animals that run into it.

Page views: 2,861  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

#  [Rust Wiki](/rust/)

[Home](/rust/) / [Barbed Wooden Barricade](/rust/item/barricade.woodwire)

  * [ __View](/rust/item/barricade.woodwire)
  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/barricade.woodwire~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/barricade.woodwire~history)



# Barbed Wooden Barricade

# Description __

The barbed wooden barricade is the second tier of barricades that will damage other players. It can be placed on foundations, and floors. They deal more damage than the wooden barricades but less than the metal barricade. Also, you can get the bleeding effect when you touch them. Trying to deal damage with melee attacks will damage you as if you ran into them.

# General Information __

  * **Identifier:** 1382263453
  * **Stack Size:** 10
  * **Despawn Time:** 20 min
  * **HP:** 400
  * **Decay Time:** 8 hours
  * **Recycler Yield:** 150x Wood 25x Metal Fragments & %50 chance to get rope.



# Blueprint Requirements __

Tool | Requirements  
---|---  
Research Table | Barbed Wooden Barricade & 75 Scrap  
Workbench Level 1 | 370 Scrap Total  
  
# Repairing And Durability __

  * **Max Repair Cost:** 146x Wood 29x Metal Fragments (Garry's Mod Tool Gun or Hammer)

Weapon | Shots | Time | Sulfur  
---|---|---|---  
Double Barrel Shotgun 12 Gauge Incendiary Shell | ~ 4 | 19 sec | 780  
Eoka Pistol 12 Gauge Incendiary Shell | ~ 4 | 21 sec | 780  
Waterpipe Shotgun 12 Gauge Incendiary Shell | ~ 4 | 26 sec | 780  
(And various other weapons) |  |  |   
  
# Crafting __

## Workbench __

This item needs to be crafted at a Workbench level 1 and requires blueprint.

Items | Quantity  
---|---  
Wood | 300x  
Metal Fragments | 50x  
Rope | 1x  
Time | 730 sec  
  
# Tips and Strategies __

  * The barbed wooden barricade can be used to block pathways and deal damage to enemies.
  * Be cautious when using melee attacks against it, as it will cause damage to you.
  * It can be a useful tool for controlling movement in a base or during a raid.

  * [ __History](/rust/item/bbq~history)



# Barbeque

# Description __

A makeshift Barbeque. You can cook significant amounts of food with this.

## Crafting Costs __

  * x40 Metal Fragments
  * x100 Wood



## Recycling Output __

  * x20 Metal Fragments
  * x50 Wood



# Repair Costs __

Tool Used | Repair Cost | Condition Loss | Blueprint Requirement  
---|---|---|---  
Hammer | x21 Metal Frags + x49 Wood | - | NO  
Garry's Mod Tool Gun | x21 Metal Frags + x49 Wood | - | NO  
Repair Bench | x8 Metal Frags + x20 Wood | 20% | NO  
  
Page views: 7,250  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Raw Bear Meat

# Description __

Raw Bear Meat. Eating it will damage your health, try cooking it first.

Page views: 2,388  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Cooked Bear Meat

# Description __

Delicious Bear Meat, Eating it will restore some health, hunger, and thirst.

Updated: A Long Time Ago
